msg:To clarify: the hotel shuttle bus is only responsible for sending guests from the lobby to the hotel's main gate near Shendi West Road, not to the Disney entrance as other guests on Dianping generally introduced. The shuttle bus ride takes about one minute.
The hotel combines Spanish style with Shanghai-style garden architecture, quiet and elegant. But the garden is a low shrub, and when there is plenty of sunlight, there are no tall trees to provide shade, so it will be more sunny.
The room air conditioner leaks: Shanghai's night weather is cooler during the stay, and the hotel air conditioner cannot heat alone. After turning off the central air conditioner in the room, there is still a perceptible cool breeze blowing in, and there is a leakage phenomenon. (The skylight is closed)
The washbasin is narrow and there is no trash can. The closest one is in the bathroom behind you. Because there is a door that needs to be opened and closed, it is very inconvenient to throw away the garbage for washing.
The breakfast is very exquisite, but there are many people going to Disney in the morning, which will be noisy!

Breakfast is here in the lobby. It seems small, but if you really want to Everything you want is there, and the taste is pretty good...

Highly recommended, I will stay here again when I go to Disneyland next time
